<h1 _ngcontent-csh-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="Image"> Image </h1>

<div _ngcontent-csh-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>Image为图片组件，常用于在应用中显示图片。Image支持加载<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-image-pixelmap">PixelMap</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resourcestr">ResourceStr</a>和<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#drawabledescriptor10">DrawableDescriptor</a>类型的数据源，支持png、jpg、jpeg、bmp、svg、webp、gif和heif类型的图片格式，不支持apng和svga格式。</p>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <p>该组件从API version 7开始支持。后续版本如有新增内容，则采用上角标单独标记该内容的起始版本。</p>      <p>使用快捷组合键对Image组件复制时，Image组件必须处于获焦状态，如何获焦请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-common-events-focus-event#设置组件是否可获焦" target="_blank">设置组件是否可获焦</a>。Image组件默认不获焦，需将<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-focus#focusable">focusable</a>属性设置为true，即可使用Tab键将焦点切换到组件上，再将<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-focus#focusontouch9">focusOnTouch</a>属性设置为true，即可实现点击获焦。</p>      <p>图片格式支持SVG图源，SVG标签文档请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-svg">SVG标签说明</a>。</p>      <p>动图的播放依赖于Image节点的可见性变化，其默认行为是不播放的。当节点可见时，通过回调启动动画，当节点不可见时，停止动画。可见性状态的判断是通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-component-visible-area-change-event#onvisibleareachange">onVisibleAreaChange</a>事件触发的，当可见阈值ratios大于0时，表明Image处于可见状态。</p>      <p>如果图片加载过程中出现白色块，请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/best-practices/bpta-image-white-lump-solution" target="_blank">Image白块问题解决方案</a>。如果图片加载时间过长，请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/best-practices/bpta-texture-compression-improve-performance" target="_blank">预置图片资源加载优化</a>。</p>     </div></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 182px;">     <h2 id="需要权限" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">需要权限<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="需要权限" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>使用网络图片时，需要申请权限ohos.permission.INTERNET。具体申请方式请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/declare-permissions" target="_blank">声明权限</a>。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 182px;">     <h2 id="子组件" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">子组件<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="子组件" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>无</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 146px;">     <h2 id="接口" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">接口<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="接口" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>         <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2105px;">     <h3 id="image-1" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">Image<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="image-1" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>Image(src: PixelMap | ResourceStr | DrawableDescriptor)</p>     <p>通过图片数据源获取图片，用于后续渲染展示。</p>     <p>Image组件加载图片失败或图片尺寸为0时，图片组件大小自动为0，不跟随父组件的布局约束。</p>     <p>Image组件默认按照居中裁剪，例如组件宽高设置相同，原图长宽不等，此时按照中间区域进行裁剪。</p>     <p>Image加载成功且组件不设置宽高时，其显示大小自适应父组件。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.11.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.11.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.11.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.11.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">src</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-image-common#pixelmap">PixelMap</a> | <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resourcestr">ResourceStr</a>| <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#drawabledescriptor10">DrawableDescriptor</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>图片的数据源，支持本地图片和网络图片，引用方式请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-graphics-display#加载图片资源" target="_blank">加载图片资源</a>。</p>          <p>1. PixelMap格式为像素图，常用于图片编辑的场景。</p>          <p>2. ResourceStr包含Resource和string格式。</p>          <p>string格式可用于加载网络图片和本地图片，常用于加载网络图片。当<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#示例25使用相对路径显示图片">使用相对路径引用本地图片</a>时，不支持跨包/跨模块调用该Image组件，建议使用Resource格式来管理需全局使用的图片资源。</p>          <p>- 支持Base64字符串。</p>          <p>- 传入的字符串为https网络图片地址时，建议参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#示例2下载与显示静态网络图片">示例2下载与显示静态网络图片</a>。</p>          <p>- 支持file://路径前缀的字符串，应用沙箱URI：file://&lt;bundleName&gt;/&lt;sandboxPath&gt;。应用沙箱路径URI构造可参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-file-fileuri#constructor10">constructor</a>。沙箱路径需要使用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-file-fileuri#fileurigeturifrompath">fileUri.getUriFromPath(path)</a>方法将路径转换为应用沙箱URI，然后传入显示。同时需要保证目录包路径下的文件有可读权限。</p>          <p>Resource格式可以跨包/跨模块访问资源文件，是访问本地图片的推荐方式，具体示例参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/resource-categories-and-access#跨haphsp包应用资源" target="_blank">跨HAP/HSP包应用资源</a>。</p>          <p>3. 当传入资源id或name为普通图片时，生成DrawableDescriptor对象。传入<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkui-drawabledescriptor#animateddrawabledescriptor12">AnimatedDrawableDescriptor</a>类型可播放PixelMap数组动画。</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>- ArkTS卡片上支持gif图片格式动效，但仅在显示时播放一次。</p>          <p>- ArkTS卡片上不支持http://等网络相关路径前缀和file://路径前缀的字符串。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>Image直接传入URL可能会带来的潜在性能问题，例如：(1) 大图加载时无法提前下载，白块显示的时间较长；(2) 小图设置同步加载，在弱网环境下，可能会阻塞UI线程造成冻屏问题；(3) 在快速滑动的瀑布流中，无法提前对即将要显示的图片进行下载，导致滑动白块较多。不同场景下，性能问题会有不同的表现，建议将网络下载部分与Image的显示剥离，可提前下载或者异步下载。如果图片加载过程中出现白色块，请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/best-practices/bpta-image-white-lump-solution" target="_blank">Image白块问题解决方案</a>。如果图片加载时间过长，请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/best-practices/bpta-texture-compression-improve-performance" target="_blank">预置图片资源加载优化</a>。</p>       <p>src由有效值（可正常解析并加载的图片资源）切换为无效值（无法解析或加载的图片路径）时，组件应保持显示此前成功加载的图片内容，不进行清除或重置操作。</p>       <p>当Image组件入参为<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-image-pixelmap">PixelMap</a>类型时，只有当PixelMap对象的引用发生变化（即指向一个新的PixelMap实例），Image组件才能感知到数据的变化。仅修改PixelMap对象的内容（如像素值）而不更换对象引用，无法触发数据变化的感知。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 877px;">     <h3 id="image12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">Image<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="image12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>Image(src: PixelMap | ResourceStr | DrawableDescriptor | ImageContent)</p>     <p>src新增<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#imagecontent12">ImageContent</a>类型，可指定对应的图形内容。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">src</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-image-common#pixelmap">PixelMap</a> | <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resourcestr">ResourceStr</a>| <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#drawabledescriptor10">DrawableDescriptor</a>| <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#imagecontent12">ImageContent</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>图片的数据源，支持本地图片和网络图片，引用方式请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-graphics-display#加载图片资源" target="_blank">加载图片资源</a>。</p>          <p>PixelMap、ResourceStr和DrawableDescriptor的使用请参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#image-1">Image</a>的scr参数说明。</p>          <p>传入<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#imagecontent12">ImageContent</a>类型，指定图像内容。</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>- ArkTS卡片上支持gif图片格式动效，但仅在显示时播放一次。</p>          <p>- ArkTS卡片上不支持http://等网络相关路径前缀和file://路径前缀的字符串。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 874px;">     <h3 id="image12-1" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">Image<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="image12-1" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>Image(src: PixelMap | ResourceStr | DrawableDescriptor, imageAIOptions: ImageAIOptions)</p>     <p>Image新增<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-image-common#imageaioptions12">imageAIOptions</a>参数，为组件设置AI分析选项。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">src</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-image-common#pixelmap">PixelMap</a> | <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resourcestr">ResourceStr</a>| <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#drawabledescriptor10">DrawableDescriptor</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>图片的数据源，支持本地图片和网络图片，引用方式请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-graphics-display#加载图片资源" target="_blank">加载图片资源</a>。</p>          <p>PixelMap、ResourceStr和DrawableDescriptor的使用请参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#image-1">Image</a>的scr参数说明。</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>- ArkTS卡片上支持gif图片格式动效，但仅在显示时播放一次。</p>          <p>- ArkTS卡片上不支持http://等网络相关路径前缀和file://路径前缀的字符串。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">imageAIOptions</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-image-common#imageaioptions12">ImageAIOptions</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">给组件设置一个AI分析选项，通过此项可配置分析类型或绑定一个分析控制器。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 274px;">     <h2 id="属性" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">属性<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="属性" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>属性的详细使用指导请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-graphics-display#添加属性" target="_blank">添加属性</a>。除支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-component-general-attributes">通用属性</a>外，还支持以下属性：</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>Image组件不支持设置通用属性<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-foreground-color#foregroundcolor">foregroundColor</a>，可以通过Image组件的<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#fillcolor">fillColor</a>属性设置填充颜色。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1197px;">     <h3 id="alt" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">alt<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="alt" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>alt(value: string | Resource | PixelMap)</p>     <p>设置图片加载过程中显示的占位图。</p>     <p>占位图支持使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#objectfit">objectFit</a>设置填充效果，与图片的填充效果一致。</p>     <p>当组件的参数类型为<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkui-drawabledescriptor#animateddrawabledescriptor12">AnimatedDrawableDescriptor</a>时设置该属性不生效。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.10.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.10.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.10.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.10.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string | <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resource">Resource</a> | <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-image-pixelmap">PixelMap</a><sup>12+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置图片加载过程中显示的占位图，支持本地图片（png、jpg、bmp、svg、gif和heif类型），支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-image-pixelmap">PixelMap</a>类型图片，不支持网络图片。</p>          <p>- 支持Base64字符串。</p>          <p>- 支持file://路径前缀的字符串，应用沙箱URI：file://&lt;bundleName&gt;/&lt;sandboxPath&gt;。应用沙箱路径URI构造可参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-file-fileuri#constructor10">constructor</a>。沙箱路径需要使用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-file-fileuri#fileurigeturifrompath">fileUri.getUriFromPath(path)</a>方法将路径转换为应用沙箱URI，然后传入显示。同时需要保证目录包路径下的文件有可读权限。</p>          <p>默认值：null</p>          <p>由有效值（可正常解析并加载的图片资源）切换为无效值（无法解析或加载的图片路径）时，组件保持显示此前成功加载的图片内容，不进行清除或重置操作。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div   <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 589px;">     <h3 id="imagematrix15" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">imageMatrix<sup>15+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="imagematrix15" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>imageMatrix(matrix: ImageMatrix)</p>     <p>设置图片的变换矩阵。通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#imagematrix15对象说明">ImageMatrix</a>对象使用平移、旋转、缩放等函数，实现宫格缩略图的最佳呈现。SVG类型图源不支持该属性。</p>     <p>设置resizable、objectRepeat属性时，该属性设置不生效。该属性只针对图源做处理，不会触发Image组件的回调事件。</p>     <p>该属性与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#objectfit">objectFit</a>属性强关联，仅在<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#objectfit">objectFit</a>属性设置为<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-appendix-enums#imagefit">ImageFit</a>.MATRIX时生效。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span <p>图片组件已设置width、height属性时，fitOriginalSize属性不生效。</p>     <p>当组件的参数类型为<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkui-drawabledescriptor#animateddrawabledescriptor12">AnimatedDrawableDescriptor</a>时设置该属性不生效。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.10.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.10.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.10.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.10.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>图片的显示尺寸是否跟随图源尺寸。</p>          <p>默认值：false</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>当不设置fitOriginalSize或者设置fitOriginalSize为false时，组件显示大小不跟随图源大小。</p>          <p>当设置fitOriginalSize为true时，组件显示大小跟随图源大小。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 877px;">     <h3 id="fillcolor" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">fillColor<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.19.9.1.5.1.1"        </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1093px;">     <h3 id="autoresize" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">autoResize<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="autoresize" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>autoResize(value: boolean)</p>     <p>设置图片解码过程中是否对图源自动缩放。降采样解码时图片的部分信息丢失，因此可能会导致图片质量的下降（如：出现锯齿），这时可以选择把autoResize设为false，按原图尺寸解码，提升显示效果，但会增加内存占用。</p>     <p>原图尺寸和显示尺寸不匹配时，图片都会出现些许的失真、模糊。最佳清晰度配置建议：</p>     <p>图片缩小显示时：.autoResize(false) + .interpolation(.Medium)</p>     <p>图片放大显示时：.interpolation(.High)</p>     <p>当组件的参数类型为<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkui-drawabledescriptor#animateddrawabledescriptor12">AnimatedDrawableDescriptor</a>和SVG时设置该属性不生效。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.22.12.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.22.12.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.22.12.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.22.12.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>图片解码过程中是否对图源自动缩放。设置为true时，组件会根据显示区域的尺寸决定用于绘制的图源尺寸，有利于减少内存占用。如原图大小为800x1200，而显示区域大小为200x200，则图片会降采样解码到200x300的尺寸（实际计算过程中会依赖缩放和填充类型的配置，从而得到的计算结果会有差异），从而大幅度节省图片占用的内存。</p>          <p>默认值：false，false表示关闭图源自动缩放，true表示开启图源自动缩放。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 829px;">     <h3 id="syncload8" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">syncLoad<sup>8+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="syncload8" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>syncLoad(value: boolean)</p>     <p>设置是否同步加载图片。建议加载尺寸较小的本地图片时将syncLoad设为true，因为耗时较短，在主线程上执行即可。</p>     <p>当组件的参数类型为<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkui-drawabledescriptor#animateddrawabledescriptor12">AnimatedDrawableDescriptor</a>时设置该属性不生效。</p>     <p>如果加载图片时出现闪烁，设置syncLoad为true。详情请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/best-practices/bpta-click-to-click-response-optimization#section715115119192" target="_blank">并发优化</a>。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.23.10.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.23.10.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.23.10.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.23.10.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>是否同步加载图片，默认是异步加载。同步加载时阻塞UI线程，不会显示占位图。</p>          <p>默认值：false，false表示异步加载图片，true表示同步加载图片。</p>          <p>阻塞主线程超过6s将导致AppFreeze，具体参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/appfreeze-guidelines" target="_blank">AppFreeze（应用冻屏）检测</a>。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 613px;">     <h3 id="copyoption9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">copyOption<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="copyoption9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>copyOption(value: CopyOptions)</p>     <p>设置图片是否可复制。当copyOption设置为非CopyOptions.None时，支持使用长按、鼠标右击、快捷组合键'CTRL+C'等方式进行复制。SVG图片不支持复制。</p>     <p>当组件的参数类型为<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkui-drawabledescriptor#animateddrawabledescriptor12">AnimatedDrawableDescriptor</a>时设置该属性不生效。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.24.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.24.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.24.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.24.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder"     <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>图片是否可复制。</p>          <p>默认值：CopyOptions.None</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1655px;">     <h3 id="colorfilter9" anchorid="colorfilter9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>colorFilter(value: ColorFilter | DrawingColorFilter)</p>     <p>为图像设置颜色滤镜效果。</p>     <p>设置该属性时，<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#rendermode">renderMode</a>属性设置不生效。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.25.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.25.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.25.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.25.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#colorfilter9">ColorFilter</a> | <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#drawingcolorfilter12">DrawingColorFilter<sup>12+</sup></a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>1. 给图像设置颜色滤镜效果，入参为一个的4x5的RGBA转换矩阵。</p>          <p>2. 从API version12开始支持@ohos.graphics.drawing的ColorFilter类型作为入参。</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>API version 11及之前，SVG类型图源不支持该属性。</p>          <p>从API version 12开始，该接口中的DrawingColorfilter类型支持在元服务中使用。其中，SVG类型的图源只有设置了stroke属性（无论是否有值）才会生效。</p>          <p>从API version 21开始，当<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#supportsvg221">supportSvg2</a>属性设置为true时，colorFilter属性对整个SVG图源起作用。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p>颜色滤镜通过一个4x5的矩阵来设置图像的颜色滤镜，矩阵第一行表示R（红色）的向量值，第二行表示G（绿色）的向量值，第三行表示B（蓝色）的向量值，第四行表示A（透明度）的向量值，4行分别代表不同的RGBA的向量值。</p>     <p>当矩阵对角线值为1，其余值为0时，保持图片原有色彩。</p>     <p><strong>计算规则：</strong></p>     <p>如果输入的滤镜矩阵如下（其中矩阵值的范围[0, 1]）：</p>     <p><span><img originheight="123" originwidth="207" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251211115415.34226228320958364635155635517076:50001231000000:2800:D37EBAF6C0FB3F70DAD785C4C91341CA25E269971A8ECE0D221BCE8ACFA93ACF.png" class="notEnlarge" width="207" height="123"></span></p>     <p>像素点为[R, G, B, A]，色值的范围[0, 255]</p>     <p>则过滤后的颜色为 [R’, G’, B’, A’]</p>     <p><span><img originheight="127" originwidth="324" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251211115416.22037417461102050691669954511968:50001231000000:2800:0904B0F4A8CA0A3D4B7F7800540D5089E925CC864E7CD4C9839F37D785D1D05F.png" width="324" height="127"></span></p>     <p>该属性的具体使用可以参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#示例9为图像设置颜色滤镜效果">示例9</a>。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 685px;">     <h3 id="draggable9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">draggable<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="draggable9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>draggable(value: boolean)</p>     <p>设置组件默认拖拽效果。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>组件默认拖拽效果，设置为true时，组件可拖拽，绑定的长按手势不生效。</p>          <p>API version 9及之前，默认值为false。API version 10及之后，默认值为true。</p>          <p>若用户需要设置自定义手势，则需要将draggable设置为false。设置为false之后，拖拽类事件不再触发。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 985px;">     <h3 id="enableanalyzer11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">enableAnalyzer<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="enableanalyzer11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>enableAnalyzer(enable: boolean)</p>     <p>设置组件支持AI分析，当前支持主体识别、文字识别和对象查找等功能。具体使用指导请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/vision-imageanalyzer" target="_blank">AI识图</a>。</p>     <p>不能和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-overlay">overlay</a>属性同时使用，两者同时设置时overlay中<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#custombuilder8">CustomBuilder</a>属性将失效。该特性依赖设备能力。</p>     <p>分析图像要求是静态非矢量图，即svg、gif等图像类型不支持分析，支持传入<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-image-pixelmap">PixelMap</a>进行分析，目前仅支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-image-e#pixelmapformat7">RGBA_8888</a>类型，使用方式见<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#示例5开启图像ai分析">示例5开启图像AI分析</a>。</p>     <p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#alt">alt</a>占位图不支持分析，<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#objectrepeat">objectRepeat</a>属性仅在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-appendix-enums#imagerepeat">ImageRepeat</a>.NoRepeat下支持分析，隐私遮罩属性<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-obscured">obscured</a>打开时不支持分析。</p>     <p>基于完整原始图像进行分析，设置<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-sharp-clipping#clip12">clip</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-size#margin">margin</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-border#borderradius">borderRadius</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-location#position">position</a>和<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#objectfit">objectFit</a>属性导致图像显示不完整，或使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#rendermode">renderMode</a>设置蒙层，仍基于完整原始图像进行分析。 <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#copyoption9">copyOption</a>属性不影响AI分析功能。</p>     <p>当组件的参数类型为<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkui-drawabledescriptor#animateddrawabledescriptor12">AnimatedDrawableDescriptor</a>时设置该属性不生效。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>         <p>需要配置权限：ohos.permission.INTERNET。</p></li>        <li>         <p>从API version 12开始，该接口支持在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-attribute-modifier#attributemodifier">attributeModifier</a>中调用。</p></li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.13.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.13.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.13.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.13.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">enable</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>Image组件是否支持AI分析。</p>          <p>设置为true时，Image组件支持AI分析。设置为false时，Image组件不支持AI分析。</p>          <p>默认值：false</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="resizable11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#resizableoptions11">ResizableOptions</a> 时，objectRepeat属性和orientation属性设置不生效。</p>     <p>当设置 top +bottom 大于原图的高或者 left + right 大于原图的宽时 <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#resizableoptions11">ResizableOptions</a> 属性设置不生效。</p>     <p>当组件的参数类型为<a </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 805px;">     <h3 id="orientation14" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">orientation<sup>14+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="orientation14" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>orientation(orientation: ImageRotateOrientation)</p>     <p>设置图像内容的显示方向。</p>     <p>该属性对<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#alt">alt</a>占位图不生效。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 14开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.31.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.31.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left"   <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">orientation</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#imagerotateorientation14">ImageRotateOrientation</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>图像内容的显示方向。</p>          <p>仅支持静态位图的显示。</p>          <p>如果需要显示携带旋转角度信息或翻转信息的图片，建议使用ImageRotateOrientation.AUTO进行设置。</p>          <p>默认值：ImageRotateOrientation.UP</p>          <p>设置为undefined或null时，取值为ImageRotateOrientation.AUTO。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 757px;">     <h3 id="hdrbrightness19" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">hdrBrightness<sup>19+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="hdrbrightness19" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>hdrBrightness(brightness: number)</p>     <p>设置组件在显示HDR图片时的亮度。</p>     <p>SVG类型图源不支持该属性。</p>     <p>该属性与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#dynamicrangemode12">dynamicRangeMode</a>属性同时设置时，<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#dynamicrangemode12">dynamicRangeMode</a>属性不生效。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 19开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th   <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">brightness</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>用于调整组件展示HDR图片的亮度，该接口仅对HDR图源生效。</p>          <p>默认值：1.0</p>          <p>取值范围：[0.0，1.0]，小于0和大于1.0时取1。0表示图片按照SDR亮度显示，1表示图片按照当前允许的最高HDR亮度显示。</p></td> id="mcps1.3.38.5.1.6.1.1" width="20%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.38.5.1.6.1.2" width="20%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#edgewidths9">EdgeWidths</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>边框宽度类型，用于描述组件边框不同方向的宽度。</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>只有当bottom和right同时大于0时，该属性生效。</p>          <p>当设置了top时，图片顶部拉伸，图片的像素值保持不变。</p>          <p>当设置了right时，图片右部拉伸，图片的像素值保持不变。</p>          <p>当设置了bottom时，图片底部拉伸，图片的像素值保持不变。</p>          <p>当设置了left时，图片左部拉伸，图片的像素值保持不变。</p>          <p>每个方向的宽度默认值为0，传入数字时默认单位为vp。</p>          <p>设置了EdgeWidths后的效果如图1（设置EdgeWidths效果图）所示。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">lattice<sup>12+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#drawinglattice12">DrawingLattice</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>矩形网格对象。</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>通过@ohos.graphics.drawing的createImageLattice接口创建Lattice类型作为入参。将图像划分为矩形网格，同时处于偶数列和偶数行上的网格图像是固定的，不会被拉伸。</p>          <p>该参数对<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-background#backgroundimageresizable12">backgroundImageResizable</a>接口不生效。</p>          <p>传入数字时默认单位为px。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>图1</strong> 设置EdgeWidths效果图</p>     <p><span><img originheight="230" originwidth="547" SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.5.1.4.1.1" class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2253px;">     <h3 id="oncomplete" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">onComplete<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="oncomplete" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>onComplete(callback: (event?: { width: number, height: number, componentWidth: number, componentHeight: number, loadingStatus: number,contentWidth: number, contentHeight: number, contentOffsetX: number, contentOffsetY: number }) =&gt; void)</p>     <p>图片数据加载成功和解码成功时均触发该回调，返回成功加载的图片尺寸。</p>     <p>当组件的参数类型为<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkui-drawabledescriptor#animateddrawabledescriptor12">AnimatedDrawableDescriptor</a>时该事件不触发。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p> class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="onfinish" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>onFinish(event: () =&gt; void)</p>     <p>当加载的源文件为带动效的SVG格式图片时，SVG动效播放完成时会触发这个回调。如果动效为无限循环动效，则不会触发这个回调。</p>     <p>仅支持SVG格式的图片。当组件的参数类型为<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkui-drawabledescriptor#animateddrawabledescriptor12">AnimatedDrawableDescriptor</a>时该事件不触发。</p>     </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p>以下是错误信息的详细介绍：ImageError的error属性为错误信息对象，其中code为错误码，message为错误信息。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table> anchor-icon-link" anchorid="示例2下载与显示静态网络图片" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>加载网络图片时，默认网络超时是5分钟，建议使用alt配置加载时的占位图。使用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/http-request" target="_blank">HTTP</a>工具包发送网络请求，接着将返回的数据解码为Image组件中的PixelMap，加载gif到PixelMap时，gif显示为静态图。图片开发可参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/image-overview" target="_blank">图片处理</a>。</p>     <p>使用网络图片时，需要申请权限ohos.permission.INTERNET。具体申请方式请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/declare-permissions" target="_blank">声明权限</a>。</p>     <div _ngcontent-csh-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-csh-c106="" class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="示例3下载与显示网络gif图片" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>该示例使用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-request-cachedownload#cachedownloaddownload">cacheDownload.download</a>接口下载网络gif图片。</p>     <p>使用网络图片时，需要申请权限ohos.permission.INTERNET。具体申请方式请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/declare-permissions" target="_blank">声明权限</a>。</p>     <div class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-csh-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-csh-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-csh-c106="" class="handle-button </li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-variable constant_">TAG</span> = <span class="hljs-string">'AceImage'</span>;</li><li>

class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="示例22获取图片的exif信息并设置图像内容的显示方向" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>该示例通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-image-imagesource#getimageproperty11">getImageProperty</a>接口，获取图片的exif信息，再根据获取到的exif信息，通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#orientation14">orientation</a>属性设置图像内容显示为正确方向。</p>     <div _ngcontent-csh-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div </li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@Entry</span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@Component</span></li><li>struct <span class="hljs-title class_">Example</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-meta">@State</span> <span class="hljs-attr">rotateOrientation</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">ImageRotateOrientation</span> = <span class="hljs-title class_">ImageRotateOrientation</span>.<span class="hljs-property">UP</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-meta">@State</span> <span class="hljs-attr">pixelMap</span>: image.<span class="hljs-property">PixelMap</span> | <span class="hljs-literal">undefined</span> = <span class="hljs-literal">undefined</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-meta">@State</span> <span class="hljs-attr">text1</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">'The exif orientation is '</span>;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-meta">@State</span> <span class="hljs-attr">text2</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">string</span> = <span class="hljs-string">'Set orientation to '</span>;</li><li>
</li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">// 根据获取到的EXIF方向信息，转换ImageRotateOrientation，使图片显示为正确的方向。</span></li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">getOrientation</span>(<span
